Vai--Unicode-block structured-concept-Mcs
block.U+A500|42240|ꔀ..U+A63F|42559|꘿

McsHitp-creation:: {2018-09-15},

overview of U+A500..U+A63F

description::
× Unicode-block-name: Vai
× range: U+A500|42240|ꔀ..U+A63F|42559|꘿
× plane: plane.0
× quantity-of-code-points: 320
× quantity-of-chars: 300
× script: Vai
· The name "Lisu" is preferred by the user community. Many linguists also use the name "Fraser" or "Fraser Lisu". Used for the Old Lisu orthography.
[https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Unicode_character_property#Block]
[ftp://www.unicode.org/Public/UCD/latest/ucd/]
